Configuration hot-reload system for FORGE.\n//!\n//! This module provides real-time configuration reloading without restarting forge.\n//! It watches `~/.forge/config.yaml` for changes and applies them immediately.\n//!\n//! ## Hot-Reload Targets\n//!\n//! 1. **Theme changes** - Immediate visual update (< 500ms)\n//! 2. **Hotkey bindings** - Immediate (next keypress)\n//! 3. **Refresh intervals** - Within 1 second\n//! 4. **Budget thresholds** - Within 1 second\n//! 5. **Model tier mappings** - Within 5 seconds\n//!\n//! ## Architecture\n//!\n//! - Uses `notify` crate for file system watching (reuses existing watcher pattern)\n//! - Debounces rapid changes (50ms default)\n//! - Validates config before applying\n//! - Graceful degradation on invalid config (keeps old config)\n//! - Emits events for UI updates\n\nuse std::path::PathBuf;\nuse std::sync::mpsc::{Receiver, Sender};\nuse std::time::Duration;\n\nuse notify::{Event, EventKind, RecommendedWatcher, RecursiveMode, Watcher};\nuse tracing::{debug, info, warn};\n\n// Re-export config types from forge-config crate\npub use forge_config::{ForgeConfig, ConfigLoadError, config_path};\n\n/// Default debounce duration for config changes (50ms).\npub const DEFAULT_DEBOUNCE_MS: u64 = 50;\n\n/// Configuration events emitted when config changes.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum ConfigEvent {\n    /// Config file was modified and successfully reloaded.\n    Reloaded {\n        /// New configuration values\n        config: ForgeConfig,\n    },\n    /// Config file was modified but validation failed.\n    ValidationError {\n        /// Error message describing what's wrong\n        error: String,\n        /// Path to the config file\n        path: PathBuf,\n    },\n    /// Config file was created (first time).\n    Created {\n        /// Initial configuration\n        config: ForgeConfig,\n    },\n    /// Config file was deleted.\n    Removed,\n    /// Error reading or parsing config file.\n    Error {\n        /// Error message\n        error: String,\n    },\n}\n\n/// Configuration watcher that monitors config.yaml for changes.\n///\n/// Uses the `notify` crate to watch for file system events and emits\n/// `ConfigEvent`s when the config file changes.\npub struct ConfigWatcher {\n    /// The underlying file watcher\n    _watcher: RecommendedWatcher,\n\n    /// Config file path being watched\n    config_path: PathBuf,\n\n    /// Current configuration\n    current_config: ForgeConfig,\n\n    /// Stop signal sender\n    _stop_tx: Sender<()>,\n}\n\nimpl ConfigWatcher {\n    /// Create a new config watcher with default settings.\n    ///\n    /// Returns the watcher and a receiver for config events.\n    pub fn new() -> Option<(Self, Receiver<ConfigEvent>)> {\n        let config_path = config_path()?;\n        Self::with_path(config_path)\n    }\n\n    /// Create a config watcher for a specific path.\n    pub fn with_path(config_path: PathBuf) -> Option<(Self, Receiver<ConfigEvent>)> {\n        // Load initial config\n        let current_config = ForgeConfig::load_from(&config_path).unwrap_or_default();\n\n        let (event_tx, event_rx) = std::sync::mpsc::channel();\n        let (stop_tx, _stop_rx) = std::sync::mpsc::channel();\n\n        // Create file watcher\n        let config_path_clone = config_path.clone();\n        let event_tx_clone = event_tx.clone();\n\n        let mut watcher = RecommendedWatcher::new(\n            move |result: std::result::Result<Event, notify::Error>| {\n                match result {\n                    Ok(event) => {\n                        // Check if this is our config file\n                        if !event.paths.iter().any(|p| p == &config_path_clone) {\n                            return;\n                        }\n\n                        match event.kind {\n                            EventKind::Create(_) | EventKind::Modify(_) => {\n                                // Small delay to ensure file is fully written\n                                std::thread::sleep(Duration::from_millis(50));\n\n                                match ForgeConfig::load_from(&config_path_clone) {\n                                    Some(new_config) => {\n                                        // Validate before emitting\n                                        match new_config.validate() {\n                                            Ok(()) => {\n                                                let is_create = matches!(event.kind, EventKind::Create(_));\n                                                let event_type = if is_create {\n                                                    ConfigEvent::Created { config: new_config }\n                                                } else {\n                                                    ConfigEvent::Reloaded { config: new_config }\n                                                };\n                                                if event_tx_clone.send(event_type).is_err() {\n                                                    debug!(\"Failed to send config event - channel closed\");\n                                                }\n                                            }\n                                            Err(e) => {\n                                                if event_tx_clone\n                                                    .send(ConfigEvent::ValidationError {\n                                                        error: e,\n                                                        path: config_path_clone.clone(),\n                                                    })\n                                                    .is_err()\n                                                {\n                                                    debug!(\"Failed to send validation error - channel closed\");\n                                                }\n                                            }\n                                        }\n                                    }\n                                    None => {\n                                        if event_tx_clone\n                                            .send(ConfigEvent::Error {\n                                                error: \"Failed to parse config file\".to_string(),\n                                            })\n                                            .is_err()\n                                        {\n                                            debug!(\"Failed to send error event - channel closed\");\n                                        }\n                                    }\n                                }\n                            }\n                            EventKind::Remove(_)\n                                if event_tx_clone.send(ConfigEvent::Removed).is_err() => {\n                                    debug!(\"Failed to send remove event - channel closed\");\n                                }\n                            _ => {}\n                        }\n                    }\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        warn!(\"Config watcher error: {:?}\", e);\n                    }\n                }\n            },\n            notify::Config::default().with_poll_interval(Duration::from_millis(DEFAULT_DEBOUNCE_MS)),\n        )\n        .ok()?;\n\n        // Watch the parent directory (more reliable than watching file directly)\n        let watch_path = config_path.parent().unwrap_or(&config_path);\n        watcher.watch(watch_path, RecursiveMode::NonRecursive).ok()?;\n\n        info!(\"Started watching config file: {:?}\", config_path);\n\n        let watcher = Self {\n            _watcher: watcher,\n            config_path,\n            current_config,\n            _stop_tx: stop_tx,\n        };\n\n        Some((watcher, event_rx))\n    }\n\n    /// Get the current configuration.\n    pub fn current_config(&self) -> &ForgeConfig {\n        &self.current_config\n    }\n\n    /// Get the config file path.\n    pub fn config_path(&self) -> &PathBuf {\n        &self.config_path\n    }\n\n    /// Update the current config (called after handling an event).\n    pub fn update_config(&mut self, config: ForgeConfig) {\n        self.current_config = config;\n    }\n}\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n temp_dir.path().join(\"config.yaml\");\n\n        // Create initial config\n        let initial_content = r#\"\ndashboard:\n  refresh_interval_ms: 1000\n\"#;\n        fs::write(&config_path, initial_content).unwrap();\n\n        let (watcher, rx) = ConfigWatcher::with_path(config_path.clone()).unwrap();\n\n        // Give watcher time to initialize\n modified_content).unwrap();\n\n        // Wait for event\n        std::thread::sleep(Duration::from_millis(200));\n\n        // Check for event\n        let event = rx.try_recv();\n        match event               // Some systems emit create instead of modify\n                assert_eq!(config.dashboard.refresh_interval_ms, 500);\n            }\n            other => {\n                // Event  },\n55\t\n56\t    /// Config validation failed\n57\t    #[error(\"Config validation failed: {0}\")]\n58\t    ValidationError(String),\n59\t}\n60\t\n61\timpl From<String> for ConfigLoadError {\n62\t If the file\n151\t    /// doesn't exist, is unreadable, or contains invalid YAML, it returns\n152\t    /// the default configuration rather than failing.\n153\t    ///\n154\t    /// Errors are logged but don't prevent the application from starting.\n155\t    pub fn load_from(path: &PathBuf) -> Option<Self> {\n156\t        if !path.exists() {\n157\t            tracing::debug!(\"Config file does not exist: {:?} - using defaults\", path);\n158\t            return None;\n159\t        }\n160\t\n161\t        // Try to read the file\n162\t        let content = match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {\n163\t            Ok(c) => c,\n164\t            Err(e) => {\n165\t                tracing::warn!(\n166\t                    path = ?path,\n167\t                    error = %e,\n168\t                    \"Failed to read config file - using defaults\"\n169\t                );\n170\t                return None;\n171\t            }\n172\t        };\n173\t\n174\t        // Try to parse with fallback to partial parsing\n175\t        Self::parse_with_fallback(&content)\n176\t    }\n177\t\n178\t    /// Load configuration from a specific path with detailed error reporting.\n179\t    ///\n180\t    /// Returns a Result with detailed error information for display to users.\n181\t    pub fn load_from_with_error(path: &PathBuf) -> Result<Self, ConfigLoadError> {\n182\t        if !path.exists() {\n183\t            return Err(ConfigLoadError::NotFound(path.clone()));\n184\t        }\n185\t\n186\t        // Try to read the file\n187\t        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(path)\n188\t            .map_err(|e| ConfigLoadError::ReadError {\n189\t                path: path.clone(),\n190\t                error: e,\n191\t            })?;\n192\t\n193\t        // Try to parse as full YAML\n194\t        match serde_yaml::from_str::<ForgeConfig>(&content) {\n195\t            Ok(config) => {\n196\t                // Validate and return errors if invalid\n197\t                config.validate()?;\n198\t                Ok(config)\n199\t            }\n200\t            Err(e) => Err(ConfigLoadError::ParseError {\n201\t                path: path.clone(),\n202\t                error: e,\n203\t            }),\n204\t        }\n205\t    }\n206\t\n207\t    /// Parse configuration from YAML string.\n208\t    ///\n209\t    /// Returns None if parsing fails completely.\n210\t    pub fn parse(content: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n211\t        Self::parse_with_fallback(content)\n212\t    }\n213\t\n214\t    /// Parse configuration with fallback for partial/invalid configs.\n215\t    ///\n216\t    /// This method:\n217\t    /// 1. Tries to parse the full config\n218\t    /// 2. Falls back to partial parsing if sections are invalid\n219\t    /// 3. Returns default for completely invalid YAML\n220\t    fn parse_with_fallback(content: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n221\t        // First try to parse as full YAML\n222\t        match serde_yaml::from_str::<ForgeConfig>(content) {\n223\t            Ok(config) => {\n224\t                // Validate and warn about issues, but still return the config\n225\t                if let Err(e) = config.validate() {\n226\t                    tracing::warn!(\n227\t                        error = %e,\n228\t                        \"Config validation warning - some settings may be ignored\"\n229\t                    );\n230\t                }\n231\t                tracing::debug!(\"Successfully parsed forge config\");\n232\t                Some(config)\n233\t            }\n234\t            Err(e) => {\n235\t                // Format detailed error message with line/column information\n236\t                let error_msg = format_yaml_error(&e);\n237\t                tracing::warn!(\n238\t                    error = %error_msg,\n239\t                    \"Failed to parse config YAML - attempting partial parse\"\n240\t                );\n241\t\n242\t                // Try to parse individual sections as a fallback\n243\t                Self::parse_partial(content)\n244\t            }\n245\t        }\n246\t    }\n247\t\n248\t    /// Attempt to parse individual sections of a malformed config.\n249\t    ///\n250\t    /// This allows partial configs to work even if one section has errors.\n251\t    fn parse_partial(content: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n252\t   tracing::warn!(\n257\t                    error = %e,\n258\t                    \"Config is not valid YAML - using defaults\"\n259\t                );\n260\t                return None;\n261\t            }\n262\t        };\n263\t\n264\t        // Try to extract individual sections\n265\t        let dashboard = yaml\n266\t            .get(\"dashboard\")\n267\t            .and_then(|v|      })\n305\t    }\n306\t\n307\t    /// Validate the configuration.\n308\t    ///\n309\t    /// Returns Ok(()) if valid, Err with message if invalid.\n310\t    /// Warnings are logged but don't cause validation failure.\n311\t    pub fn validate(&self) -> Result<(), String> {\n312\t        let mut warnings = Vec::new();\n313\t\n314\t        // Validate refresh interval (must be >= 100ms)\n315\t self.dashboard.refresh_interval_ms\n319\t            ));\n320\t        }\n321\t\n322\t        // Validate max_fps (must be 1-120)\n323\t        if self.dashboard.max_fps == 0 || self.dashboard.max_fps self.cost_tracking.budget_critical_threshold\n342\t            ));\n343\t        }\n344\t\n345\t        // Validate theme name if specified\n346\t        if let Some(ref theme_name) = self.theme.name }\n384\t    }\n385\t\n386\t    /// Sanitize the configuration by fixing invalid values.\n387\t    ///\n388\t    /// Returns a new config with all invalid values replaced by defaults.\n389\t    pub fn Configuration management for FORGE.\n//!\n//! This crate handles loading, validating, and managing FORGE configuration\n//! from `~/.forge/config.yaml`.\n\nuse std::io;\nuse std::path::PathBuf;\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse thiserror::Error;\n\n/// Default config file path (~/.forge/config.yaml).\npub fn config_path() -> Option<PathBuf> {\n    dirs::home_dir().map(|h| h.join(\".forge/config.yaml\"))\n}\n\n/// Format a YAML parse error with line/column information if available.\nfn format_yaml_error(error: &serde_yaml::Error) -> String {\n    if let Some(location) = error.location() {\n        format!(\n            \"YAML parse error at line {}, column {}: {}\",\n            location.line(),\n            location.column(),\n            error\n        )\n    } else {\n        format!(\"YAML parse error: {}\", error)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Errors that can occur when loading configuration.\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum ConfigLoadError {\n    /// Could not determine home directory\n    #[error(\"Could not determine home directory\")]\n    NoHomePath,\n\n    /// Config file not found\n    #[error(\"Config file not found: {0}\")]\n    NotFound(PathBuf),\n\n    /// Error reading config file\n    #[error(\"Failed to read config file {path}: {error}\")]\n    ReadError {\n        path: PathBuf,\n        #[source]\n        error: io::Error,\n    },\n\n    /// Error parsing YAML\n    #[error(\"Failed to parse config YAML in {path}: {}\", format_yaml_error(error))]\n    ParseError {\n        path: PathBuf,\n        error: serde_yaml::Error,\n    },\n\n    /// Config validation failed\n    #[error(\"Config validation failed: {0}\")]\n    ValidationError(String),\n}\n\nimpl From<String> for ConfigLoadError {\n    fn from(s: String) -> Self {\n        ConfigLoadError::ValidationError(s)\n    }\n}\n\nimpl ConfigLoadError {\n    /// Get the line number where the error occurred (if available).\n    pub fn line_number(&self) -> Option<usize> {\n        match self {\n            ConfigLoadError::ParseError { error, .. } => {\n                error.location().map(|loc| loc.line())\n            }\n            _ => None,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the column number where the error occurred (if available).\n    pub fn column_number(&self) -> Option<usize> {\n        match self {\n            ConfigLoadError::ParseError { error, .. } => {\n                error.location().map(|loc| loc.column())\n            }\n            _ => None,\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the config file path (if applicable).\n    pub fn path(&self) -> Option<&PathBuf> {\n        match self {\n            ConfigLoadError::NotFound(path)\n            | ConfigLoadError::ReadError { path, .. }\n            | ConfigLoadError::ParseError { path, .. } => Some(path),\n            _ => None,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Forge configuration structure.\n///\n/// This represents the subset of config.yaml that can be hot-reloaded.\n/// Changes to these fields will take effect immediately.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default, Deserialize, Serialize, PartialEq)]\npub struct ForgeConfig {\n    /// Dashboard configuration\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub path (~/.forge/config.yaml).\n    ///\n    /// Returns default configuration if the file doesn't exist or is invalid.\n    /// Invalid configs are logged as warnings but don't prevent startup.\n    pub fn load() -> Option<Self> {\n        let path = config_path()?;\n        Self::load_from(&path)\n    }\n\n    /// Load configuration from the default path with detailed error reporting.\n    ///\n    /// Returns a Result with detailed error information for display to users.\n    pub fn load_with_error() -> Result<Self, ConfigLoadError> {\n        let path = config_path().ok_or(ConfigLoadError::NoHomePath)?;\n        Self::load_from_with_error(&path)\n    }\n\n    /// Load configuration from a specific path with graceful fallback.\n    ///\n    /// This method attempts to load and parse the config file. If the file\n    /// doesn't exist, is unreadable, or contains invalid YAML, it returns\n    /// the default configuration rather than failing.\n    ///\n    /// Errors are logged but don't prevent the application from starting.\n    pub fn load_from(path: &PathBuf) -> Option<Self> {\n        if !path.exists() {\n            tracing::debug!(\"Config file does not exist: {:?} - using defaults\", path);\n            return None;\n        }\n\n        // Try to read the file\n        let content = match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {\n            Ok(c) => c,\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(\n                    path = ?path,\n                    error = %e,\n                    \"Failed to read config file - using defaults\"\n                );\n                return None;\n            }\n        };\n\n        // Try to parse with fallback to partial parsing\n        Self::parse_with_fallback(&content)\n    }\n\n    /// Load configuration from a specific path with detailed error reporting.\n    ///\n    /// Returns a Result with detailed error information for display to users.\n    pub fn load_from_with_error(path: &PathBuf) -> Result<Self, ConfigLoadError> {\n        if !path.exists() {\n            return Err(ConfigLoadError::NotFound(path.clone()));\n        }\n\n        // Try to read the file\n        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(path)\n            .map_err(|e| ConfigLoadError::ReadError {\n                path: path.clone(),\n                error: e,\n            })?;\n\n        // Try to parse as full YAML\n        match serde_yaml::from_str::<ForgeConfig>(&content) {\n            Ok(config) => {\n                // Validate and return errors if invalid\n                config.validate()?;\n                Ok(config)\n            }\n            Err(e) => Err(ConfigLoadError::ParseError {\n                path: path.clone(),\n                error: e,\n            }),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Parse configuration from YAML string.\n    ///\n    /// Returns None if parsing fails completely.\n    pub fn parse(content: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n        Self::parse_with_fallback(content)\n    }\n\n    /// Parse configuration with fallback for partial/invalid configs.\n    ///\n    /// This method:\n    /// 1. Tries to parse the full config\n    /// 2. Falls back to partial parsing if sections are invalid\n    /// 3. Returns default for completely invalid YAML\n    fn parse_with_fallback(content: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n        // First try to parse as full YAML\n        match serde_yaml::from_str::<ForgeConfig>(content) {\n            Ok(config) => {\n                // Validate and warn about issues, but still return the config\n                if let Err(e) = config.validate() {\n                    tracing::warn!(\n                        error = %e,\n                        \"Config validation warning - some settings may be ignored\"\n                    );\n                }\n                tracing::debug!(\"Successfully parsed forge config\");\n                Some(config)\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                // Format detailed error message with line/column information\n                let error_msg = format_yaml_error(&e);\n                tracing::warn!(\n                    error = %error_msg,\n                    \"Failed to parse config YAML - attempting partial parse\"\n                );\n\n                // Try to parse individual sections as a fallback\n                Self::parse_partial(content)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Attempt to parse individual sections of a malformed config.\n    ///\n    /// This allows partial configs to work even if one section has errors.\n    fn parse_partial(content: &str) -> Option<Self> {\n        // Try to parse as generic YAML first\n        let yaml: serde_yaml::Value = match serde_yaml::from_str(content) {\n            Ok(y) => y,\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(\n                    error = %e,\n                    \"Config is not valid YAML - using defaults\"\n                );\n                return None;\n            }\n        };\n\n        // Try to extract individual sections\n        let dashboard = yaml\n            .get(\"dashboard\")\n            .and_then(|v| serde_yaml::from_value(v.clone()).ok())\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n        let theme = yaml\n            .get(\"theme\")\n            .and_then(|v| serde_yaml::from_value(v.clone()).ok())\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n        let cost_tracking = yaml\n            .get(\"cost_tracking\")\n            .and_then(|v| serde_yaml::from_value(v.clone()).ok())\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n        let auto_recovery = yaml\n            .get(\"auto_recovery\")\n            .and_then(|v| serde_yaml::from_value(v.clone()).ok())\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n        let workers = yaml\n            .get(\"workers\")\n            .and_then(|v| serde_yaml::from_value(v.clone()).ok())\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n        let notifications = yaml\n            .get(\"notifications\")\n            .and_then(|v| serde_yaml::from_value(v.clone()).ok())\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n        tracing::info!(\"Loaded partial config - some sections may use defaults\");\n\n        Some(Self {\n            dashboard,\n            theme,\n            cost_tracking,\n            auto_recovery,\n            workers,\n            notifications,\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Validate the configuration.\n    ///\n    /// Returns Ok(()) if valid, Err with message if invalid.\n    /// Warnings are logged but don't cause validation failure.\n    pub fn validate(&self) -> Result<(), String> {\n        let mut warnings = Vec::new();\n\n        // Validate refresh interval (must be >= 100ms)\n        if self.dashboard.refresh_interval_ms < 100 {\n            warnings.push(format!(\n                \"refresh_interval_ms {} is too low, using minimum of 100ms\",\n                self.dashboard.refresh_interval_ms\n            ));\n        }\n\n        // Validate max_fps (must be 1-120)\n        if self.dashboard.max_fps == 0 || self.dashboard.max_fps > 120 {\n            warnings.push(format!(\n                \"max_fps {} is invalid, must be between 1 and 120\",\n                self.dashboard.max_fps\n            ));\n        }\n\n        // Validate budget thresholds (must be 0-100)\n        if self.cost_tracking.budget_warning_threshold > 100 {\n            warnings.push(format!(\n                \"budget_warning_threshold {} exceeds 100%\",\n                self.cost_tracking.budget_warning_threshold\n            ));\n        }\n\n        if self.cost_tracking.budget_critical_threshold > 100 {\n            warnings.push(format!(\n                \"budget_critical_threshold {} exceeds 100%\",\n                self.cost_tracking.budget_critical_threshold\n            ));\n        }\n\n        // Validate theme name if specified\n        if let Some(ref theme_name) = self.theme.name {\n            let valid_themes = [\"default\", \"dark\", \"light\", \"cyberpunk\"];\n            if !valid_themes.contains(&theme_name.to_lowercase().as_str()) {\n                warnings.push(format!(\n                    \"Invalid theme '{}', valid themes: {:?}\",\n                    theme_name, valid_themes\n                ));\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Validate max workers\n        if self.workers.max_workers == 0 {\n            warnings.push(\"max_workers must be at least 1\".to_string());\n        }\n\n        // Validate default model\n        let valid_models = [\"sonnet\", \"opus\", \"haiku\", \"glm\"];\n        if !valid_models.contains(&self.workers.default_model.to_lowercase().as_str()) {\n            warnings.push(format!(\n                \"Invalid default_model '{}', valid models: {:?}\",\n                self.workers.default_model, valid_models\n            ));\n        }\n\n        // Validate sonnet costs (must be non-negative)\n        if self.cost_tracking.sonnet_cost_per_1k_input < 0.0 {\n            warnings.push(\"sonnet_cost_per_1k_input must be non-negative\".to_string());\n        }\n        if self.cost_tracking.sonnet_cost_per_1k_output < 0.0 {\n            warnings.push(\"sonnet_cost_per_1k_output must be non-negative\".to_string());\n        }\n\n        if warnings.is_empty() {\n            Ok(())\n        } else {\n            // Return the first warning as the error message\n            Err(warnings.join(\"; \"))\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Sanitize the configuration by fixing invalid values.\n    ///\n    /// Returns a new config with all invalid values replaced by defaults.\n    pub fn sanitized(&self) -> Self {\n        let mut config = self.clone();\n\n        // Sanitize refresh interval\n        if config.dashboard.refresh_interval_ms < 100 {\n            tracing::warn!(\n                original = config.dashboard.refresh_interval_ms,\n                \"Sanitizing refresh_interval_ms to minimum 100ms\"\n            );\n            config.dashboard.refresh_interval_ms = 100;\n        }\n\n        // Sanitize max_fps\n        if config.dashboard.max_fps == 0 || config.dashboard.max_fps > 120 {\n            tracing::warn!(\n                original = config.dashboard.max_fps,\n                \"Sanitizing max_fps to default 60\"\n            );\n            config.dashboard.max_fps = 60;\n        }\n\n        // Sanitize budget thresholds\n        if config.cost_tracking.budget_warning_threshold > 100 {\n            tracing::warn!(\n                original = config.cost_tracking.budget_warning_threshold,\n                \"Sanitizing budget_warning_threshold to 100\"\n            );\n            config.cost_tracking.budget_warning_threshold = 100;\n        }\n\n        if config.cost_tracking.budget_critical_threshold > 100 {\n            tracing::warn!(\n                original = config.cost_tracking.budget_critical_threshold,\n                \"Sanitizing budget_critical_threshold to 100\"\n            );\n            config.cost_tracking.budget_critical_threshold = 100;\n        }\n\n        // Sanitize theme name\n        if let Some(ref theme_name) = config.theme.name {\n            let valid_themes = [\"default\", \"dark\", \"light\", \"cyberpunk\"];\n            if !valid_themes.contains(&theme_name.to_lowercase().as_str()) {\n                tracing::warn!(\n                    original = theme_name,\n                    \"Sanitizing invalid theme name to default\"\n                );\n                config.theme.name = None;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Sanitize max workers\n        if config.workers.max_workers == 0 {\n            tracing::warn!(\n                original = config.workers.max_workers,\n                \"Sanitizing max_workers to minimum 1\"\n            );\n            config.workers.max_workers = 1;\n        }\n\n        // Sanitize default model\n        let valid_models = [\"sonnet\", \"opus\", \"haiku\", \"glm\"];\n        if !valid_models.contains(&config.workers.default_model.to_lowercase().as_str()) {\n            tracing::warn!(\n                original = config.workers.default_model,\n                \"Sanitizing invalid default_model to sonnet\"\n            );\n            config.workers.default_model = \"sonnet\".to_string();\n        }\n\n        // Sanitize sonnet costs\n        if config.cost_tracking.sonnet_cost_per_1k_input < 0.0 {\n            config.cost_tracking.sonnet_cost_per_1k_input = 0.003;\n        }\n        if config.cost_tracking.sonnet_cost_per_1k_output < 0.0 {\n            config.cost_tracking.sonnet_cost_per_1k_output = 0.015;\n        }\n\n        config\n    }\n\n    /// Save configuration to a file.\n    ///\n    /// Writes the configuration as YAML to the specified path.\n    /// Creates parent directories if they don't exist.\n    pub fn save_to(&self, path: &PathBuf) -> Result<(), ConfigLoadError> {\n        // Create parent directory if needed\n        if let Some(parent) = path.parent()\n            && !parent.exists() {\n                std::fs::create_dir_all(parent).map_err(|e| ConfigLoadError::ValidationError(\n                    format!(\"Failed to create config directory: {}\", e)\n                ))?;\n        }\n\n        // Serialize to YAML\n        let yaml = serde_yaml::to_string(self)\n            .map_err(|e| ConfigLoadError::ValidationError(\n                format!(\"Failed to serialize config: {}\", e)\n            ))?;\n\n        // Write to file\n        std::fs::write(path, yaml)\n            .map_err(|e| ConfigLoadError::ValidationError(\n                format!(\"Failed to write config file: {}\", e)\n            ))?;\n\n        tracing::info!(\"Saved configuration to {:?}\", path);\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Save configuration to the default path (~/.forge/config.yaml).\n    pub fn save(&self) -> Result<(), ConfigLoadError> {\n        let path = config_path().ok_or(ConfigLoadError::NoHomePath)?;\n        self.save_to(&path)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Dashboard configuration.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize, Serialize, PartialEq)]\npub struct #[serde(default = \"default_max_fps\")]\n    pub max_fps: u64,\n\n    /// Default layout mode.\n    #[serde(default = \"default_layout\")]\n    pub default_layout: String,\n\n    /// Log retention Self {\n            refresh_interval_ms: default_refresh_interval(),\n            max_fps: default_max_fps(),\n            default_layout: default_layout(),\n            log_retention_days: default_log_retention_days(),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn default_refresh_interval() -> u64 {\n    1000\n}\n\nfn default_max_fps() -> u64 {\n    60\n}\n\nfn default_layout() -> String {\n    \"overview\".to_string()\n}\n\nfn default_log_retention_days() -> u64 {\n    7\n}\n\n/// Theme configuration.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default, Deserialize, Serialize, PartialEq)]\npub struct \"sonnet\".to_string()\n}\n\n/// Cost tracking configuration.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Deserialize, Serialize, PartialEq)]\npub struct CostTrackingConfig {\n    /// Whether cost tracking is enabled.\n    #[serde(default = \"default_cost_enabled\")]\n    pub enabled: bool,\n\n    /// Budget warning threshold (percentage).\n    #[serde(default = \"default_warning_threshold\")]\n    pub
